<time>1615606610078< /time><Review>I was dogsitting my brother's puppers and she was anxious about being in an unfamiliar place and also had an irritating ear infection. My brother recommended CBD. I found BayQueen carried pet CBD especially in tincture form which I heard good reviews about. I placed an order about ~10-15 min before closing time. I thought they would process my order the next morning which was fine and I was expecting that. <Time>1608149267408<//Time><rating>5</rating>< text>
BACKGROUND:  In July 2020, the driver side back tire blew out causing some major damage to the back of my car.  It did cut through wires, but I had not known what other damage it might have caused.

My car was doing well until one day, the sound of the door being ajar would not stop ringing, there was an awful smell coming from the car, and the car was making a weird sound.  That is when I sent out one of those Yelp thingies to the various places about car repair.

- - - - - - - - - - -

Albeit I got a number of responses to my Yelp thingie, I started reading through each of their reviews.  Supreme Auto had amazing reviews and I think I liked that fact it was not a big commercialized place.  In one of the reviews, someone mentioned that it was a family shop and I wanted to support local shops as much as possible.

- - - - - - - - -

When I got to Supreme Auto Repair, I met Sam.  He was very nice and understanding.  I told him the whole story.  He listened.  It took one day but a complete diagnosis was completed.  I came back the next day and he explained what the major needs of the car was in order to get it back on the freeway.  I looked at the pricing and was shocked because I was being quoted about 4x more at Calibre Collision for some of the work.

I will never forget what he had to say about the wiring: "It is not rocket science if you know what you are doing, so it should not cost hundreds of dollars."  Calibre had quoted me literally $1,000+ just for the wiring alone.

I did the SNAP Loan thing which was annoying because the numbers were not working.  HOWEVER, Sam was calm, cool, and collective, while I was a panicking mess.  He was like, "Don't worry, we'll get it to work."  Which we eventually did.... Talk about a professional!

He did share that a lot of the repairs were because maintenance was not performed regularly.  He explained that even though I kept up with maintenance when I got the car, my aunt and her family had not.  Thus these issues would have surfaced one way or another.  This brought such a relief to me as I thought it was due to the tire blowing incident.

When I took the car home that same day, I noticed that the smell was gone, the door ajar ringing was gone, and the car was running smoother than when I first brought it in.  However, taking Sam's recommendation, I took the side streets home.  This time, I did not have to stop every so many miles to give the car a rest.  I think they had already done some work on my car!  Whoa!!  I doubt a car dealership or Calibre would have done that!!

- - - - - - - - - - -

The following week, I took the car in for its repair.  It took the weekend, and I got the car back on Monday (if I remember correctly).  He did share that they did a final look over to see what else needed to be fixed.  There was just one more thing.  However, he guaranteed me that I could take the car on the freeway, that I would be able to visit my family in Los Angeles, and I should not worry.  In fact, he told me to take the freeway home.  That's how confident he was in the work of his employees!

Since seeing him, I have been to LA twice and on the freeway many times.  Oh!  And I now know what 3rd gear feels like.  3rd gear wasn't working on the car before!!

- - - - - - - -

Sam and his crew are very professional, nice, humble, and industrious.  I think the operative word here is humble. They get the work done.  They go above and beyond to make sure you are satisfied.

So the question is: would I return to Supreme Auto Repair and Alignment?  ABSOLUTELY!!  They have not only earned my business but also my loyalty!!

Thanks Sam and the Crew!!  You all are the best!!</text>

<Text>My Grandfather William Thomas Perry Jr. was an aeroplane mechanic who worked in North American in World War 2. Received his certificate in Oklahoma right before he moved to California with wife in 1942. He was in the Merchant Marines for approximately for three weeks then his supervisor found out that he had an certificate in aeroplane mechanic training school. They told him that he was needed at North American in 1942 because he had skills and experience as a mechanic and completed his vocational training in that field and because of his training my Grandfather was abled to transfer to enter into North American.

< review>
I was lucky enough to tour the entire facility here and was completely blown away. This place is amazing, even just from the outside and just getting on the grounds and seeing the rocket out front was amazing. I won't say what's inside to any detail, but there are officially released pictures of the facility you can Google to give you an idea of what it looks like. < review>
Sunday Oct 7 became a historic evening for my wife and I.
While seated on our patio in Indio, California enjoying the nighttime Southern skies a very bright object appeared from behind the Santa Rosa Mountains and suddenly unbeknownst to us we were witnessing our first ever live space Rocket launch! It was ducking in and out of unseen clouds so it was difficult to figure out what was taking place. The white trail behind it turned orange which I now assume occurred when the booster engine was jettisoned. The Rocket emerged from the clouds and filled the heavens with an eerie super bright light. Wow, it was spectacular! We are totally uninformed and surprised at what is going on in the Aerospace Industry anywhere but especially
here in California! I did some catching up. So Spacex sends their reusable Falcon Rocket into space to place a satellite into orbit and then it and the reusable 1st booster engine return to Vandenberg AFB to land at their original launch site! A first for them on the West Coast. Congratulations, it‚Äôs Unreal‚ÄºÔ∏èWhen I was a kid our family huddled around a 1929 Vacuum Tube radio for our entertainment. Today what Spacex is accomplishing is out of this World!<//review>
